FNV PBR PPLIGHTING REMAINING MATERIAL ARRAY CONSUMER FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which BA9EE0 draw-stage helpers read +0xB0/+0xB8/+0xBC/+0xC0?
2. Are those reads real type-3 material arrays, or unrelated stack/object offsets?
3. Do remaining-array reads feed BA9EE0 resources, only branch predicates, or only serialization?
4. Is there any safe vanilla draw-stage path for normal/height/env/env-mask before visible PBR replacement?

Compatibility rule:
Visible replacement remains blocked unless every texture stage used by the replacement is proven from source array to final SetTexture.
